<div class="description">This is the date that this article will be sent via <b>IntelliNews Daily Email</b> to subscribers. Use this when publishing an intraday article which should be included in the next <b>IntelliNews Daily</b>.<br><br>
(ie. If you write this at 2PM Monday, it clearly cannot go into Mondays morning daily.  By putting in the next days date, it will be included in the next morning daily.)<br><br>
Enter the date of the INTELLINEWS DAILY MORNING EMAIL in which the article will be included.  This date will be different from the above when you are publishing an intraday article (which will be available on the Website or delivered to intraday email recipients live), but want to in Daliy email to customers. Use this when publishing an intraday article and want to resend in next Daily.</div>
</div>

<div class="filter-guidelines form-wrapper" id="edit-body-und-0-format-guidelines"><div class="filter-guidelines-item filter-guidelines-full_html"><h3>Full HTML</h3><ul class="tips"><li>Links to Twitter status updates are converted to Embedded Tweets.</li><li>You may use <a href="/filter/tips/full_html#filter-insert_view">[view:<em>name=display=args</em>] tags</a> to display views.</li><li>Web page addresses and e-mail addresses turn into links automatically.</li><li>Lines and paragraphs break automatically.</li></ul></div><div class="filter-guidelines-item filter-guidelines-plain_text"><h3>Plain text</h3><ul class="tips"><li>No HTML tags allowed.</li><li>You may use <a href="/filter/tips/plain_text#filter-insert_view">[view:<em>name=display=args</em>] tags</a> to display views.</li><li>Web page addresses and e-mail addresses turn into links automatically.</li><li>Lines and paragraphs break automatically.</li></ul></div><div class="filter-guidelines-item filter-guidelines-php_code"><h3>PHP code</h3><ul class="tips"><li>You may post PHP code. You should include &lt;?php ?&gt; tags.</li></ul></div><div class="filter-guidelines-item filter-guidelines-filtered_html"><h3>Filtered HTML</h3><ul class="tips"><li>Links to Twitter status updates are converted to Embedded Tweets.</li><li>Web page addresses and e-mail addresses turn into links automatically.</li><li>Allowed HTML tags: &lt;a&gt; &lt;em&gt; &lt;strong&gt; &lt;cite&gt; &lt;blockquote&gt; &lt;code&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;ol&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;dl&gt; &lt;dt&gt; &lt;dd&gt;</li><li>Lines and paragraphs break automatically.</li></ul></div></div></div></fieldset>

</li><li><div class='no-term-reference-tree-button'></div><div class="form-item form-type-checkbox form-item-field-industry-und-0-451-451-children-476-476-children-534-534-children-680-680">

    <span>
      
       <strong>Mortgage REIT&#039;s</strong><br><p>Companies or Trusts that service, originate, purchase and/or securitize residential and/or commercial mortgage loans.  Includes trusts that invest in mortgage-backed securities and other mortgage related assets.</p>

    </span>
</a> </label>
